[Haley] [오전 10:56] Photo
[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 3:54] 제목 [롯데하이마트-MS오피스 패키지]
[Web발신]
제품인증코드 : 44MXW-P9Y6W-3KWHP-3TMCX-439CZ

본 제품은 Microsoft Office H&S 2019 정품 소프트웨어입니다.

마이크로소프트의 소프트웨어 판매 정책상 아래와 같은 유의점 참조 바랍니다.

1. 본 제품은 일반 소비자 구매용으로 재판매가 불가능합니다.
2. 제품인증코드 등록 후에는 반품이 불가능합니다.
3. 30일 이상 미등록시 반품이 불가능합니다.

설치방법안내
1. www.office.com/setup 접속
2. Microsoft 계정 로그인 (없을경우 생성필수)
3. 제품 키(25자리) 입력
4. 국가 또는 지역, 언어 선택후 '다음'
5. Office 다운로드하여 설치

발송시간 : 2020년 02월 25일 14시 00분
[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 3:54] Photo
[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 11:42] desc;

CREATE TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO(
    CUSTOMER_KINDOF_LOGIN   VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_ID             VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_PWD            VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_NAME           VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_PHONE          VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_ADDR           VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_NICKNAME       VARCHAR(60),
    CUSTOMER_RANK           NUMBER,
    CUSTOMER_DATE           DATE
);
ALTER TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO 
ADD (CUSTOMER_KINDOF_LOGIN  VARCHAR(60));

SELECT * FROM CUSTOMER_INFO;
COMMIT;
DESC CUSTOMER_INFO;

CREATE TABLE VIDEO_INFO(
    VIDEO_SEQ_ID            NUMBER,
    VIDEO_NAME              VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_COUNTRY    VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_CITY       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_DAYS       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_WITH       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_WEATHER    VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_ADDRESS           VARCHAR2(150),
    VIDEO_CUSTOMER_ID       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_DATE              DATE,
    VIDEO_VIEW_COUNT        NUMBER,
    VIDEO_GOOD_COUNT        NUMBER
);
SELECT * FROM VIDEO_INFO;
COMMIT;

CREATE TABLE ORDERLIST_INFO(
    ORDERLIST_CUSTOMER_ID   VARCHAR2(60),
    ORDERLIST_UPLOADER_ID   VARCHAR2(60),
    ORDERLIST_COUNT         NUMBER,
    ORDERLIST_CATEGORY_NAME VARCHAR2(60)
);
SELECT * FROM ORDERLIST_INFO;
COMMIT;

CREATE TABLE CATEGORY_INFO(
    CATEGORY_NAME   VARCHAR2(60)
);
SELECT * FROM CATEGORY_INFO;
COMMIT;

<script>
   var area;
   var ctx;
   var oldBcgColor = "#ff99cc";
   var oldTxtColor = "#ff6666";
   var oldStrkColor = "#9999ff";
   var canvas, drop;

   function initiateCanvas(){
      area = document.getElementById("canvas");
      ctx = area.getContext("2d");
      ctx.clearRect(0,0,500,300);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.rect(0,0,500,300);
      ctx.strokeStyle = "#9999ff";
      ctx.fillStyle = "#ff99cc";
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.stroke();
       
       area.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
           var inputVal = document.getElementById("inputtext").value;
           
           var posx=e.pageX-area.offsetLeft;   
           var posy=e.pageY-area.offsetTop;
           
           ctx.font = "30px Arial";
           ctx.fillStyle = oldTxtColor;
           ctx.fillText(inputVal, posx, posy);
            
      });
      initiateEvt();
   }
   function remove() {
      ctx.clearRect(0,0,670,370); // 픽셀 정리
   }
   function saves() {   
       alert(area.toDataURL()); 
       localStorage.setItem("canvas", area.toDataURL());    
   }
   function restore(){
      var img = new Image();
       img.src = localStorage.getItem("canvas");
       img.onload = function() { 
          ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);        
       }
   }
   
   //----------------------------------------------------------------
   
    function initiateEvt(){
     var images=document.querySelectorAll('#picturesbox > img');
     for(var i=0; i<images.length; i++){
       images[i].addEventListener('dragstart', dragged, false);
       images[i].addEventListener('dragend', ending, false);
     }

     area.addEventListener('dragover', function(e){ e.preventDefault(); }, false);
     area.addEventListener('drop', dropped, false);
   }
   function ending(e){
     elem=e.target;

   }
   function dragged(e){
     var elem=e.target;
     e.dataTransfer.setData('aa', elem.getAttribute('id'));
     e.dataTransfer.setDragImage(e.target, 0, 0); // Image left top
   }
   function dropped(e){
     e.preventDefault();
     var id=e.dataTransfer.getData('aa');
     var elem=document.getElementById(id);
   
     var posx=e.pageX-area.offsetLeft;   
     var posy=e.pageY-area.offsetTop;

     ctx.drawImage(elem, posx, posy, elem.width, elem.height);
   }
   
   //---------------------------------------------------------------------
   function canvasFill(color){
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.fillStyle = color;
      ctx.fillRect(0,0,500,300);
   }
   function canvasStroke(color){
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.strokeStyle = color;
      ctx.lineWidth = 5;
      ctx.strokeRect(0,0,500,300);  
   }

   
   function canvasTextColor(color){
      oldTxtColor = color;
   }
   
   document.body.onload = initiateCanvas;
   
   
</script>

<script>

  </script>

CREATE TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO(
    CUSTOMER_KINDOF_LOGIN   VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_ID             VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_PWD            VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_NAME           VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_PHONE          VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_ADDR           VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_NICKNAME       VARCHAR(60),
    CUSTOMER_RANK           NUMBER,
    CUSTOMER_DATE           DATE
);
ALTER TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO 
ADD (CUSTOMER_KINDOF_LOGIN  VARCHAR(60));

SELECT * FROM CUSTOMER_INFO;
COMMIT;
DESC CUSTOMER_INFO;

CREATE TABLE VIDEO_INFO(
    VIDEO_SEQ_ID            NUMBER,
    VIDEO_NAME              VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_COUNTRY    VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_CITY       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_DAYS       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_WITH       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_KINDOF_WEATHER    VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_ADDRESS           VARCHAR2(150),
    VIDEO_CUSTOMER_ID       VARCHAR2(60),
    VIDEO_DATE              DATE,
    VIDEO_VIEW_COUNT        NUMBER,
    VIDEO_GOOD_COUNT        NUMBER
);
SELECT * FROM VIDEO_INFO;
COMMIT;

CREATE TABLE ORDERLIST_INFO(
    ORDERLIST_CUSTOMER_ID   VARCHAR2(60),
    ORDERLIST_UPLOADER_ID   VARCHAR2(60),
    ORDERLIST_COUNT         NUMBER,
    ORDERLIST_CATEGORY_NAME VARCHAR2(60)
);
SELECT * FROM ORDERLIST_INFO;
COMMIT;

CREATE TABLE CATEGORY_INFO(
    CATEGORY_NAME   VARCHAR2(60)
);
SELECT * FROM CATEGORY_INFO;
COMMIT;

     ];

     var count = 1;
     $(".siteWrapper").css("background-image", 'url("' + urls[0] + '")');
     setInterval(function() {
       $(".siteWrapper").css("background-image", 'url("' + urls[count] + '")');
       count === urls.length - 1 ? (count = 0) : count++;
     }, 10000);
   });

<script>
const poem = `Wee T is a neew platform WebSite
   helping you to quickly make your own travel plan
   Treasure your best plan!`;

   let $poem = document.querySelector('#poem'),
       $chars = null,
       current = 0,
       stack = [],
       delayInterval = 4,
       delayIntervalId = null,
       repeatDelaySec = 7,
       repeatDelayId = null,
       autorepeat = true,
       _timer = null;


   function run_countdown(pbarEl, sec, callbackEnd, callbackStart) {
     let reverse_counter = 100,
         pbar = document.querySelector(pbarEl),
         _delay = sec * 10;
     
     if (pbar === null) {
       return;
     }
     
     pbar.style.width = '0%';
     clearInterval(_timer);
     
     if (callbackStart !== undefined && typeof callbackStart === 'function') {
       callbackStart();
     }
     
     _timer = setInterval(function() {
       let progress = (100 - --reverse_counter) + '%';

       window.requestAnimationFrame(() => pbar.style.width = progress);

       if (reverse_counter <= 0) {
         clearInterval(_timer);
         if (callbackEnd !== undefined && typeof callbackEnd === 'function') {
           callbackEnd();
         }
       }
     }, _delay);
   }

   function prepareText() {
     let poemChars = poem.split(''),
         charLen = poemChars.length,
         i;
     
     for (i = 0; i < charLen; i++) {
       if (poemChars[i] === '\n') {
         poemChars[i] = `<span class="cr">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
       } else {
         poemChars[i] = `<span class="char">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
       }
     }

     $poem.innerHTML = poemChars.join('');
     $chars = $poem.querySelectorAll('.char');
   }

   function styleColor(disturb) {
       const maxLightness = disturb ? 255 : 50,
             r = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
             g = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
             b = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness);
       return `color: rgba(${r},${g},${b},${Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5});`;
   }

   function styleFontWeight() {
     return 'font-weight:' + (Math.random() * 700 + 300) + ';';
   }

   function styleFontSize(disturb) {
     let baseSize = disturb ? 4 : 1.8,
         rndSize = disturb ? 5 : 0.6;
     return 'font-size:' + (Math.random() * rndSize + baseSize) + 'rem;';
   }

   function styleFontVariation() {
     return "font-variation-settings: 'slnt' " + (Math.random() * 15 * -1) + 
         ", 'ital' 0.5, 'CASL' " + Math.round(Math.random()) +
         // "'MONO' 1, " +
         ';';
   }

   function processStack() {
     if (stack.length) {
       let task = stack.shift();
       window.requestAnimationFrame(() => task.el.style = task.style);
     }
     
     if (stack.length) {
       delayIntervalId = window.setTimeout(processStack, delayInterval);
     } else if (autorepeat) {
       run_countdown('#pbar', repeatDelaySec, styleText);
     }
   }

   function styleText() {
     $chars.forEach((el, i) => {
       const disturb = Math.random() > 0.98; // 2% extreme values.
       let style = '';
       // style += 'color: #445;'; // Set font color the show the chars.
       style += styleFontWeight();
       style += styleFontSize(disturb);
       style += styleColor(disturb);
       style += styleFontVariation();
       stack.push({el: el, style: style});
     });
     
     processStack();
   }

   window.addEventListener('click', () => {
     // if (stack.length > 2000) {
     //   stack = [];
     // }
     if (delayIntervalId !== null) {
       window.clearTimeout(delayIntervalId);
       delayIntervalId = null;
     }
     
     if (repeatDelayId !== null) {
       window.clearTimeout(repeatDelayId);
       repeatDelayId = null;
     }
     
     stack = [];
     styleText();
   });

   function init() {
     // autorepeat = false;
     prepareText();
     styleText();
   }

   init();
</script>

<!-- oliver.yoo -->
<script>


const title = 'wee T';
const poet = 'Oliver Haley - 1991 1997';

const poem = `Wee T is a neew platform WebSite 
helping you to quickly make your own 
travel plan Treasure your best plan!`;


let $poem = document.querySelector('#poem'),
    $chars = null,
    current = 0,
    stack = [],
    delayInterval = 4,
    delayIntervalId = null,
    repeatDelaySec = 7,
    repeatDelayId = null,
    autorepeat = true,
    _timer = null;

function run_countdown(pbarEl, sec, callbackEnd, callbackStart) {
  let reverse_counter = 100,
      pbar = document.querySelector(pbarEl),
      _delay = sec * 10;
  
  if (pbar === null) {
    return;
  }
  
  pbar.style.width = '0%';
  clearInterval(_timer);
  
  if (callbackStart !== undefined && typeof callbackStart === 'function') {
    callbackStart();
  }
  
  _timer = setInterval(function() {
    let progress = (100 - --reverse_counter) + '%';

    //window.requestAnimationFrame(() => pbar.style.width = progress);

    if (reverse_counter <= 0) {
      clearInterval(_timer);
      if (callbackEnd !== undefined && typeof callbackEnd === 'function') {
        callbackEnd();
      }
    }
  }, _delay);
}

function prepareText() {
  let poemChars = poem.split(''),
      charLen = poemChars.length,
      i;
  
  for (i = 0; i < charLen; i++) {
    if (poemChars[i] === '\n') {
      poemChars[i] = `<span class="cr">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
    } else {
      poemChars[i] = `<span class="char">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
    }
  }

  $poem.innerHTML = poemChars.join('');
  $chars = $poem.querySelectorAll('.char');
}

function styleColor(disturb) {
    const maxLightness = disturb ? 255 : 50,
          r = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
          g = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
          b = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness);
    return `color: rgba(${r},${g},${b},${Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5});`;
}

function styleFontWeight() {
  return 'font-weight:' + (Math.random() * 700 + 300) + ';';
}

function styleFontSize(disturb) {
  let baseSize = disturb ? 4 : 1.8,
      rndSize = disturb ? 5 : 0.6;
  return 'font-size:' + (Math.random() * rndSize + baseSize) + 'rem;';
}

function styleFontVariation() {
  return "font-variation-settings: 'slnt' " + (Math.random() * 15 * -1) + 
      ", 'ital' 0.5, 'CASL' " + Math.round(Math.random()) +
      // "'MONO' 1, " +
      ';';
}

function processStack() {
  if (stack.length) {
    let task = stack.shift();
    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => task.el.style = task.style);
  }
  
  if (stack.length) {
    delayIntervalId = window.setTimeout(processStack, delayInterval);
  } else if (autorepeat) {
    run_countdown('#pbar', repeatDelaySec, styleText);
  }
}

function styleText() {
  $chars.forEach((el, i) => {
    const disturb = Math.random() > 0.98; // 2% extreme values.
    let style = '';
    // style += 'color: #445;'; // Set font color the show the chars.
    style += styleFontWeight();
    style += styleFontSize(disturb);
    style += styleColor(disturb);
    style += styleFontVariation();
    stack.push({el: el, style: style});
  });
  
  processStack();
}

window.addEventListener('click', () => {
  // if (stack.length > 2000) {
  //   stack = [];
  // }
  if (delayIntervalId !== null) {
    window.clearTimeout(delayIntervalId);
    delayIntervalId = null;
  }
  
  if (repeatDelayId !== null) {
    window.clearTimeout(repeatDelayId);
    repeatDelayId = null;
  }
  
  stack = [];
  styleText();
});

function init() {
  // autorepeat = false;
  prepareText();
  styleText();
}

init();

</script>
<!-- end oliver.yoo -->

<!-- oliver.yoo -->
<script>


const title = 'wee T';
const poet = 'Oliver Haley - 1991 1997';

const poem = `Wee T is a neew platform WebSite 
helping you to quickly make your own 
travel plan Treasure your best plan!`;


let $poem = document.querySelector('#poem'),
    $chars = null,
    current = 0,
    stack = [],
    delayInterval = 4,
    delayIntervalId = null,
    repeatDelaySec = 7,
    repeatDelayId = null,
    autorepeat = true,
    _timer = null;

function run_countdown(pbarEl, sec, callbackEnd, callbackStart) {
  let reverse_counter = 100,
      pbar = document.querySelector(pbarEl),
      _delay = sec * 10;
  
  if (pbar === null) {
    return;
  }
  
  pbar.style.width = '0%';
  clearInterval(_timer);
  
  if (callbackStart !== undefined && typeof callbackStart === 'function') {
    callbackStart();
  }
  
  _timer = setInterval(function() {
    let progress = (100 - --reverse_counter) + '%';

    //window.requestAnimationFrame(() => pbar.style.width = progress);

    if (reverse_counter <= 0) {
      clearInterval(_timer);
      if (callbackEnd !== undefined && typeof callbackEnd === 'function') {
        callbackEnd();
      }
    }
  }, _delay);
}

function prepareText() {
  let poemChars = poem.split(''),
      charLen = poemChars.length,
      i;
  
  for (i = 0; i < charLen; i++) {
    if (poemChars[i] === '\n') {
     // poemChars[i] = `<span class="cr">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
       poemChars[i] = '<span class="cr">' + poemChars[i] + '</span>';
    } else {
      //poemChars[i] = `<span class="char">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
       poemChars[i] = '<span class="char">'+ poemChars[i] +'</span>';
    }
  }

  $poem.innerHTML = poemChars.join('');
  $chars = $poem.querySelectorAll('.char');
}

function styleColor(disturb) {
    const maxLightness = disturb ? 255 : 50,
          r = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
          g = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
          b = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness);
    var color = 'color: rgba(' + r + ',' + g + ',' + b + ',' + (Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5) + ');';
    return color;
    //return `color: rgba(${r},${g},${b},${Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5});`;
}

function styleFontWeight() {
  return 'font-weight:' + (Math.random() * 700 + 300) + ';';
}

function styleFontSize(disturb) {
  let baseSize = disturb ? 4 : 1.8,
      rndSize = disturb ? 5 : 0.6;
  return 'font-size:' + (Math.random() * rndSize + baseSize) + 'rem;';
}

function styleFontVariation() {
  return "font-variation-settings: 'slnt' " + (Math.random() * 15 * -1) + 
      ", 'ital' 0.5, 'CASL' " + Math.round(Math.random()) +
      // "'MONO' 1, " +
      ';';
}

function processStack() {
  if (stack.length) {
    let task = stack.shift();
    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => task.el.style = task.style);
  }
  
  if (stack.length) {
    delayIntervalId = window.setTimeout(processStack, delayInterval);
  } else if (autorepeat) {
    run_countdown('#pbar', repeatDelaySec, styleText);
  }
}

function styleText() {
  $chars.forEach((el, i) => {
    const disturb = Math.random() > 0.98; // 2% extreme values.
    let style = '';
    // style += 'color: #445;'; // Set font color the show the chars.
    style += styleFontWeight();
    style += styleFontSize(disturb);
    style += styleColor(disturb);
    style += styleFontVariation();
    stack.push({el: el, style: style});
  });
  
  processStack();
}

window.addEventListener('click', () => {
  // if (stack.length > 2000) {
  //   stack = [];
  // }
  if (delayIntervalId !== null) {
    window.clearTimeout(delayIntervalId);
    delayIntervalId = null;
  }
  
  if (repeatDelayId !== null) {
    window.clearTimeout(repeatDelayId);
    repeatDelayId = null;
  }
  
  stack = [];
  styleText();
});

function init() {
  // autorepeat = false;
  prepareText();
  styleText();
}

init();

</script>
<!-- end oliver.yoo -->

<script>
   function checkLoginStatus(){
      var loginBtn = document.querySelector('#btnGoogleSignin');
      /* var nameTxt = document.querySelector('#name'); */
      if(gauth.isSignedIn.get()){
         console.log('logined');
         loginBtn.value = 'Logout';
         var profile = gauth.currentUser.get().getBasicProfile();
         console.log(profile.getName());
         /* nameTxt.innerHTML = 'Welcome <strong>' + profile.getName()+'<strong>'; */
      }else{
            console.log('logouted');
         loginBtn.value = 'Login';
         /* nameTxt.innerHTML = ''; */
      }
   }
   function init(){
      console.log('init');
      gapi.load('auth2', function() {
      /* Ready. Make a call to gapi.auth2.init or some other API */
         console.log('auth2');
         window.gauth = gapi.auth2.init({ // window.를 붙이면 전역변수가 된다.
            client_id: '905573480053-nj2mct13m72s933mfpvqb65du0hlu51u.apps.googleusercontent.com'
         })
         gauth.then(function(){
            console.log('googleAuth success');
            checkLoginStatus();
            
         }, function(){
            console.log('googleAuth fail');
         });
      });
   }
</script>

<script>


const title = 'wee T';
const poet = 'Oliver Haley - 1991 1997';

const poem = `Wee T is a neew platform WebSite 
helping you to quickly make your own 
travel plan Treasure your best plan!`;


let $poem = document.querySelector('#poem'),
    $chars = null,
    current = 0,
    stack = [],
    delayInterval = 4,
    delayIntervalId = null,
    repeatDelaySec = 7,
    repeatDelayId = null,
    autorepeat = true,
    _timer = null;

function run_countdown(pbarEl, sec, callbackEnd, callbackStart) {
  let reverse_counter = 100,
      pbar = document.querySelector(pbarEl),
      _delay = sec * 10;
  
  if (pbar === null) {
    return;
  }
  
  pbar.style.width = '0%';
  clearInterval(_timer);
  
  if (callbackStart !== undefined && typeof callbackStart === 'function') {
    callbackStart();
  }
  
  _timer = setInterval(function() {
    let progress = (100 - --reverse_counter) + '%';

    //window.requestAnimationFrame(() => pbar.style.width = progress);

    if (reverse_counter <= 0) {
      clearInterval(_timer);
      if (callbackEnd !== undefined && typeof callbackEnd === 'function') {
        callbackEnd();
      }
    }
  }, _delay);
}

function prepareText() {
  let poemChars = poem.split(''),
      charLen = poemChars.length,
      i;
  
  for (i = 0; i < charLen; i++) {
    if (poemChars[i] === '\n') {
     // poemChars[i] = `<span class="cr">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
       poemChars[i] = '<span class="cr">' + poemChars[i] + '</span>';
    } else {
      //poemChars[i] = `<span class="char">${poemChars[i]}</span>`;
       poemChars[i] = '<span class="char">'+ poemChars[i] +'</span>';
    }
  }

  $poem.innerHTML = poemChars.join('');
  $chars = $poem.querySelectorAll('.char');
}

function styleColor(disturb) {
    const maxLightness = disturb ? 255 : 50,
          r = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
          g = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness),
          b = Math.round(Math.random() * maxLightness);
    var color = 'color: rgba(' + r + ',' + g + ',' + b + ',' + (Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5) + ');';
    return color;
    //return `color: rgba(${r},${g},${b},${Math.random() * 0.5 + 0.5});`;
}

function styleFontWeight() {
  return 'font-weight:' + (Math.random() * 700 + 300) + ';';
}

function styleFontSize(disturb) {
  let baseSize = disturb ? 4 : 1.8,
      rndSize = disturb ? 5 : 0.6;
  return 'font-size:' + (Math.random() * rndSize + baseSize) + 'rem;';
}

function styleFontVariation() {
  return "font-variation-settings: 'slnt' " + (Math.random() * 15 * -1) + 
      ", 'ital' 0.5, 'CASL' " + Math.round(Math.random()) +
      // "'MONO' 1, " +
      ';';
}

function processStack() {
  if (stack.length) {
    let task = stack.shift();
    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => task.el.style = task.style);
  }
  
  if (stack.length) {
    delayIntervalId = window.setTimeout(processStack, delayInterval);
  } else if (autorepeat) {
    run_countdown('#pbar', repeatDelaySec, styleText);
  }
}

function styleText() {
  $chars.forEach((el, i) => {
    const disturb = Math.random() > 0.98; // 2% extreme values.
    let style = '';
    // style += 'color: #445;'; // Set font color the show the chars.
    style += styleFontWeight();
    style += styleFontSize(disturb);
    style += styleColor(disturb);
    style += styleFontVariation();
    stack.push({el: el, style: style});
  });
  
  processStack();
}

window.addEventListener('click', () => {
  // if (stack.length > 2000) {
  //   stack = [];
  // }
  if (delayIntervalId !== null) {
    window.clearTimeout(delayIntervalId);
    delayIntervalId = null;
  }
  
  if (repeatDelayId !== null) {
    window.clearTimeout(repeatDelayId);
    repeatDelayId = null;
  }
  
  stack = [];
  styleText();
});

function init() {
  // autorepeat = false;
  prepareText();
  styleText();
}

init();

</script>
<!-- end oliver.yoo -->

<script>
   function checkLoginStatus(){
      var loginBtn = document.querySelector('#btnGoogleSignin');
      /* var nameTxt = document.querySelector('#name'); */
      if(gauth.isSignedIn.get()){
         console.log('logined');
         loginBtn.value = 'Logout';
         var profile = gauth.currentUser.get().getBasicProfile();
         console.log(profile.getName());
         /* nameTxt.innerHTML = 'Welcome <strong>' + profile.getName()+'<strong>'; */
      }else{
            console.log('logouted');
         loginBtn.value = 'Login';
         /* nameTxt.innerHTML = ''; */
      }
   }
   function init(){
      console.log('init');
      gapi.load('auth2', function() {
      /* Ready. Make a call to gapi.auth2.init or some other API */
         console.log('auth2');
         window.gauth = gapi.auth2.init({ // window.를 붙이면 전역변수가 된다.
            client_id: '905573480053-nj2mct13m72s933mfpvqb65du0hlu51u.apps.googleusercontent.com'
         })
         gauth.then(function(){
            console.log('googleAuth success');
            checkLoginStatus();
            
         }, function(){
            console.log('googleAuth fail');
         });
      });
   }
</script>

<script>
/* ---------------------------------------------
Nav panel classic
--------------------------------------------- */

var mobile_nav = $(".mobile-nav");
var desktop_nav = $(".desktop-nav");

function init_classic_menu_resize(){
   
   // Mobile menu max height
   $(".mobile-on .desktop-nav > ul").css("max-height", $(window).height() - $(".main-nav").height() - 20 + "px");
   
   // Mobile menu style toggle
   if ($(window).width() <= 1024) {
       $(".main-nav").addClass("mobile-on");
   }
   else 
       if ($(window).width() > 1024) {
           $(".main-nav").removeClass("mobile-on");
           desktop_nav.show();
       }
}

function init_classic_menu(){

   
   // Navbar sticky
   
   $(".js-stick").sticky({
       topSpacing: 0
   });
   
   
   height_line($(".inner-nav > ul > li > a"), $(".main-nav"));
   height_line(mobile_nav, $(".main-nav"));
   
   mobile_nav.css({
       "width": $(".main-nav").height() + "px"
   });
   
   // Transpaner menu
   
   if ($(".main-nav").hasClass("transparent")){
      $(".main-nav").addClass("js-transparent"); 
   }
   
   $(window).scroll(function(){        
       
           if ($(window).scrollTop() > 10) {
               $(".js-transparent").removeClass("transparent");
               $(".main-nav, .nav-logo-wrap .logo, .mobile-nav").addClass("small-height");
           }
           else {
               $(".js-transparent").addClass("transparent");
               $(".main-nav, .nav-logo-wrap .logo, .mobile-nav").removeClass("small-height");
           }
       
       
   });
   
   // Mobile menu toggle
   
   mobile_nav.click(function(){
   
       if (desktop_nav.hasClass("js-opened")) {
           desktop_nav.slideUp("slow", "easeOutExpo").removeClass("js-opened");
           $(this).removeClass("active");
       }
       else {
           desktop_nav.slideDown("slow", "easeOutQuart").addClass("js-opened");
           $(this).addClass("active");
           
           // Fix for responsive menu
           if ($(".main-nav").hasClass("not-top")){
               $(window).scrollTo(".main-nav", "slow"); 
           }
           
       }
       
   });
   
   desktop_nav.find("a:not(.mn-has-sub)").click(function(){
       if (mobile_nav.hasClass("active")) {
           desktop_nav.slideUp("slow", "easeOutExpo").removeClass("js-opened");
           mobile_nav.removeClass("active");
       }
   });
</script>
</body>

</html>

select * from CUSTOMER_INFO;
CREATE TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO(
    CUSTOMER_KINDOF_LOGIN   VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_ID             VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_PWD            VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_NAME           VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_PHONE          VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_ADDR           VARCHAR2(60),
    CUSTOMER_NICKNAME       VARCHAR(60),
    CUSTOMER_RANK           NUMBER,
    CUSTOMER_DATE           DATE
);
ALTER TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO 
ADD (CUSTOMER_KINDOF_LOGIN  VARCHAR(60));

ALTER TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO 
ADD (CUSTOMER_SEQ_ID NUMBER);

ALTER TABLE CUSTOMER_INFO 
ADD (CUSTOMER_EMAIL VARCHAR(60));

SELECT * FROM CUSTOMER_INFO;
COMMIT;
DESC CUSTOMER_INFO;
delete from CUSTOMER_INFO where CUSTOMER_SEQ_ID = 0;

SELECT LAST_NUMBER  FROM USER_SEQUENCES WHERE SEQUENCE_NAME = 'CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ';
ALTER SEQUENCE CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ INCREMENT BY -68; -- 현재 값만큼 차감
SELECT CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ.NEXTVAL FROM DUAL;
SELECT CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ.CURRVAL FROM DUAL;
ALTER SEQUENCE CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ INCREMENT BY 1;

--sequence 생성
CREATE SEQUENCE CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ INCREMENT BY 1;
--sequence 삭제
DROP SEQUENCE CUSTOMER_INFO_SEQ;

update CUSTOMER_INFO set CUSTOMER_SEQ_ID = 0;

ALTER SEQUENCE CUSTOMER_SEQ_ID INCREMENT BY 1;

--

            // 파일 드롭 다운
            function fileDropDown() {
                var dropZone = $("#dropZone");
                //Drag기능 
                dropZone.on('dragenter', function(e) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    e.preventDefault();
                    // 드롭다운 영역 css
                    dropZone.css('background-color', '#E3F2FC');
                });
                dropZone.on('dragleave', function(e) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    e.preventDefault();
                    // 드롭다운 영역 css
                    dropZone.css('background-color', '#FFFFFF');
                });
                dropZone.on('dragover', function(e) {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    e.preventDefault();
                    // 드롭다운 영역 css
                    dropZone.css('background-color', '#E3F2FC');
                });
                dropZone.on('drop', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    // 드롭다운 영역 css
                    dropZone.css('background-color', '#FFFFFF');
    
                    var files = e.originalEvent.dataTransfer.files;
                    if (files != null) {
                        if (files.length < 1) {
                            /* alert("폴더 업로드 불가"); */
                            console.log("폴더 업로드 불가");
                            return;
                        } else {
                            selectFile(files)
                        }
                    } else {
                        alert("ERROR");
                    }
                });
            }

[Haley] [오전 4:02] package my.spring.weet;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Controller;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMethod;
import org.springframework.web.servlet.ModelAndView;

import dao.WatchDAO;
import vo.WeetVideoVO;


@Controller
public class WatchController {

      @Autowired
      WatchDAO dao;
      
      @RequestMapping(value = "/thumbsup.do", method = RequestMethod.GET)
       protected ModelAndView thumbsup(WeetVideoVO vo){
            ModelAndView mav = new ModelAndView();
            dao.thumbsup(vo);
            System.out.println(vo.getVideo_good_count());
            mav.addObject("thumbsupvo", vo.getVideo_good_count());
            mav.setViewName("watchPage");
            return mav;
       }
      
      @RequestMapping(value = "/thumbsdown.do", method = RequestMethod.GET)
      protected ModelAndView thumbsdown(WeetVideoVO vo) {
         ModelAndView mav = new ModelAndView();
            dao.thumbsdown(vo);
            System.out.println(vo.getVideo_bad_count());
            mav.addObject("thumbsdownvo", vo.getVideo_bad_count());
            mav.setViewName("watchPage");
         return mav;
      }
   
}

[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 12:44] ◾런타임 에러 이유

- 배열에 할당된 크기를 넘어서 접근했을 때
- 전역 배열의 크기가 메모리 제한을 초과할 때
- 지역 배열의 크기가 스택 크기 제한을 넘어갈 때
- 0으로 나눌 때
- 라이브러리에서 예외를 발생시켰을 때
- 재귀 호출이 너무 깊어질 때
- 이미 해제된 메모리를 또 참조할 때

[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 5:26] #remDr <- remoteDriver(remoteServerAddr = "localhost", port = 4445, browserName = "chrome")
remDr$open()
url<-'https://www.istarbucks.co.kr/store/store_map.do?disp=locale'
remDr$navigate(url)
Sys.sleep(3)

# 서울 클릭
clickSeoul <- remDr$findElement(using='css',"article > article:nth-child(4) ul > li:nth-child(1) > a")
clickSeoul$clickElement()
Sys.sleep(1)
# 전체 클릭
clickSeoul <- remDr$findElement(using='css',"#mCSB_2_container > ul > li:nth-child(1) > a")
clickSeoul$clickElement()
Sys.sleep(1)
#mCSB_3_container > ul > li:nth-child(2)
#mCSB_3_container > ul > li:nth-child(3)
#mCSB_3_container > ul > li:nth-child(4)
  # :
  # :
#mCSB_3_container > ul > li:nth-child(511)

infoArr_v <- NULL

# ------------------ 전체 매장 갯수 추출 코드
sizeCss <- "#container > div > form > fieldset > div > section > article.find_store_cont > article > article:nth-child(4) > div.loca_step3 > div.result_num_wrap > span"
size <- remDr$findElements(using='css selector', sizeCss)
limit <- sapply(size, function(x){x$getElementText()})
#str(limit)
limitCnt <- as.numeric(limit)
#str(limitCnt)
for(index in 1:limitCnt){
  # 하나의 매장의 매장 정보를 가져온다.
  selectInfo <- paste("#mCSB_3_container > ul > li:nth-child(",index,")", sep="")
  info <- remDr$findElement(using='css',selectInfo)
  infoTxt <- info$getElementText()
  infoArr <- strsplit(unlist(infoTxt), split="\n")
  # str(infoArr)
  print(infoArr)
  infoArr_v <- append(infoArr_v, unlist(infoArr))
  
  # 3개씩 스크롤 내리기
  if(index %% 3 == 0 && index != limit)
    remDr$executeScript(
      "var dom = document.querySelectorAll('#mCSB_3_container > ul > li')[arguments[0]];
    dom.scrollIntoView();", list(index))
}

[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 4:13] library(jsonlite)
searchUrl<- "https://openapi.naver.com/v1/search/news.json"
Client_ID <- "izGsqP2exeThwwEUVU3x"
Client_Secret <- "WrwbQ1l6ZI"
query <- URLencode(iconv("빅데이터","euc-kr","UTF-8"))
url <- paste0(searchUrl, "?query=", query, "&display=100")
response <- GET(url, add_headers("Content_Type" = "application/json",
                            "X-Naver-client-Id" = Client_ID, "X-naver-Client-Secret" = Client_Secret))

json_data <- content(response, type = 'text', encoding = "UTF-8")
json_obj <- fromJSON(json_data)
df <- data.frame(json_obj)
newText <- df[,5]
newText <- gsub("</?b>", "", newText)
newText <- gsub("&.+t;", "", newText)
newText
write(newText, "C:/oliver_c/Rstudy/oliver_txt/navernews.txt")

[❤ Babe Oliver ❤] [오후 8:25] #문제1
#1. 제품당 클릭 갯수에 대한 데이터를 가지고 다음 조건으로 그래프를 그린다.
#세로 바 그래프를 그리는데...             
#칼라는 terrain.colors 칼라로 설정한다.
#그래프 메인 제목 : "세로바 그래프 실습"
#clicklog1.png 에 저장한다.
data<-read.table(file="data/product_click.log")
#v1 시간 #v2는 p
product<-data$V2
barplot(table(product), main="세로바 그래프 실습", xlab="상품ID",ylab="클릭수",col=terrain.colors(10),las=2)
title(main="세로바 그래프 실습")
dev.copy(png,"clicklog1.png")
dev.off()

#문제2
#상품이 클릭된 시간 정보를 가지고 다음 조건의 그래프를 그린다.  
#파이그래프를 그리는데...            
#칼라는 자율이다. 
#그래프 메인 제목 : "파이그래프 실습"
#clicklog2.png 에 저장한다.
data<-read.table(file="data/product_click.log")
time<-data$V1
time<-as.factor(substr(time, 9, 10))
time
level <-paste(seq(0,18,1),"~",seq(1,19,1))
pie(table(time), labels=level,col=rainbow(20), main="파이그래프 실습")
dev.copy(png,"clicklog2.png")
dev.off()
